Host: localhost:8080

장바구니 상품 추가하기

요청 예시

POST /app/carts/save HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzUxMiJ9.eyJzdWIiOiJibG9nIiwicm9sZSI6bnVsbCwibmFtZSI6Imp1bmdoZWluIiwiaWQiOjEsImV4cCI6MTcxNzgwODM5MiwiZW1haWwiOiJqdW5naGVpbkBleGFtcGxlLmNvbSJ9._PEHSkY9fagoJlXiWmtmpy0_P4D5yTp0HwN5fzv46CW1741S_dDvAsvBVpUyZ9NiuDlz0YsauJrpZSR_eV6u7Q
Content-Length: 60
Host: localhost:8080

{
  "itemId" : 5,
  "quantity" : 10,
  "codiId" : null
}

요청 헤더

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/app/carts/save' -i -X POST \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJIUzUxMiJ9.eyJzdWIiOiJibG9nIiwicm9sZSI6bnVsbCwibmFtZSI6Imp1bmdoZWluIiwiaWQiOjEsImV4cCI6MTcxNzgwODM5MiwiZW1haWwiOiJqdW5naGVpbkBleGFtcGxlLmNvbSJ9._PEHSkY9fagoJlXiWmtmpy0_P4D5yTp0HwN5fzv46CW1741S_dDvAsvBVpUyZ9NiuDlz0YsauJrpZSR_eV6u7Q' \
    -d '{
  "itemId" : 5,
  "quantity" : 10,
  "codiId" : null
}'

Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Content-Length: 110
Host: localhost:8080

  "email" : "junghein@example.com",
  "nickName" : "dfdfd",
  "myName" : "dfd",
  "password" : "1234"
}

    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -d '{
  "email" : "junghein@example.com",
  "nickName" : "dfdfd",
  "myName" : "dfd",
  "password" : "1234"
}'

}
